׳”׳׳×׳‘׳•׳ ׳ ׳”׳™׳˜׳‘ ׳‘׳“׳‘׳¨׳™ ׳”׳©׳•"׳¢ ׳™׳¨׳׳”, ׳©׳›׳×׳‘ "׳¦׳¨׳™׳ ׳©׳™׳›׳•׳™׳ ׳‘׳׳‘׳•". ׳‘׳׳‘׳• ׳“׳•׳§׳, ׳•׳׳ ׳›׳×׳‘ ׳‘׳©׳›׳׳•. ׳׳”׳™ ׳›׳•׳ ׳× "׳”׳׳‘" ׳”׳׳׳•׳¨׳” ׳›׳׳? ׳¢׳ ׳™׳ ׳” ׳©׳•׳ ׳” ׳׳—׳׳•׳˜׳™׳ ׳׳›׳•׳•׳ ׳× ׳”׳©׳›׳. ׳›׳•׳•׳ ׳× ׳”׳©׳›׳ ׳¢׳ ׳™׳ ׳”, ׳׳”׳‘׳™׳ ׳”׳™׳˜׳‘ ׳₪׳™׳¨׳•׳© ׳”׳׳™׳׳™׳ ׳©׳׳•׳¦׳™׳ ׳׳₪׳™׳•. ׳׳¢׳•׳׳×׳” ׳›׳•׳•׳ ׳× ׳”׳׳‘ ׳¢׳ ׳™׳ ׳”, ׳׳—׳™׳•׳× ׳•׳׳”׳¨׳’׳™׳© ׳׳× ׳׳” ׳©׳׳•׳¦׳™׳ ׳‘׳₪׳™׳•. ׳׳ ׳”׳•׳ ׳׳©׳‘׳— ׳׳× ׳”׳‘׳•׳¨׳, ׳¢׳׳™׳• ׳׳”׳¨׳’׳™׳© ׳”׳¨׳’׳©׳” ׳©׳ ׳׳“׳ ׳”׳ ׳”׳ ׳” ׳׳¡׳₪׳¨ ׳‘׳©׳‘׳—׳• ׳©׳ ׳׳‘׳™׳•. ׳•׳׳ ׳”׳•׳ ׳׳‘׳§׳© ׳¢׳ ׳¦׳¨׳›׳™׳•, ׳¢׳׳™׳• ׳׳”׳¨׳’׳™׳© ׳”׳¨׳’׳©׳” ׳©׳ ׳¢׳ ׳™ ׳‘׳₪׳×׳—. ׳•׳›׳"׳© ׳”׳¨׳׳‘"׳ "׳•׳‘׳×׳—׳ ׳•׳ ׳™׳". ׳׳“׳ ׳¦׳¨׳™׳ ׳©׳”׳¨׳’׳©׳× ׳׳‘׳‘׳• ׳×׳×׳׳™׳ ׳¢׳ ׳”׳׳™׳׳™׳ ׳©׳׳•׳¦׳™׳ ׳׳₪׳™׳•.

׳“׳‘׳¨ ׳–׳” ׳”׳•׳ ׳‘׳›׳ ׳¢׳ ׳™׳ ׳•׳¢׳ ׳™׳ ׳‘׳¢׳•׳׳, ׳•׳›׳™׳“׳•׳¢ ׳©׳”׳¢׳•׳׳ ׳׳׳©׳•׳ ׳”׳¢׳׳, ׳©׳›׳ ׳”׳¢׳•׳׳ ׳”׳•׳ ׳”׳¡׳×׳¨ ׳׳₪׳ ׳™׳׳™׳•׳×, ׳”׳—׳™׳¦׳•׳ ׳™׳•׳× ׳”׳™׳ ׳’׳©׳׳™׳•׳× ׳•׳”׳₪׳ ׳™׳׳™׳•׳× ׳׳׳׳” ׳‘׳×׳•׳›׳ ׳¨׳•׳—׳ ׳™ ׳¢׳׳•׳§. ׳•׳׳ ׳¨׳§ ׳‘׳“׳‘׳¨׳™׳ ׳’׳©׳׳™׳™׳ ׳›׳ ׳”׳•׳, ׳׳׳ ׳׳£ ׳‘׳“׳‘׳¨׳™׳ ׳¨׳•׳—׳ ׳™׳™׳ ׳›׳’׳•׳ ׳×׳•׳¨׳” ׳•׳׳¦׳•׳•׳×, ׳׳™ ׳©׳׳ ׳™׳×׳‘׳•׳ ׳ ׳‘׳”׳ ׳׳¢׳•׳׳§׳, ׳׳ ׳”׳©׳™׳’ ׳׳׳ ׳׳× ׳”׳—׳™׳¦׳•׳ ׳™׳•׳× ׳©׳‘׳”׳. ׳•׳›׳׳•׳×׳• ׳׳—׳“ ׳©׳׳•׳׳“ ׳¡׳•׳’׳™׳ ׳‘׳׳¨׳•׳¦׳” ׳©׳׳ ׳”׳©׳™׳’ ׳›׳׳ ׳׳× ׳׳”׳•׳× ׳”׳¡׳•׳’׳™׳, ׳›׳ ׳‘׳›׳ ׳“׳‘׳¨ ׳•׳“׳‘׳¨ ׳©׳‘׳¢׳•׳׳ ׳¨׳•׳—׳ ׳™ ׳•׳’׳©׳׳™ ׳‘׳׳ ׳”׳×׳‘׳•׳ ׳ ׳•׳× ׳¢׳׳•׳§׳” ׳׳ ׳”׳©׳™׳’ ׳׳×׳•׳›׳ ׳”׳“׳‘׳¨ ׳›׳׳. ׳•׳–׳” ׳¢׳ ׳™׳ ׳• ׳©׳ ׳׳™׳׳•׳“ ׳”׳׳•׳¡׳¨, ׳׳׳׳•׳“ ׳‘׳›׳ ׳“׳‘׳¨ ׳׳× ׳”׳×׳•׳›׳ ׳”׳₪׳ ׳™׳׳™  ׳©׳׳•, ׳•׳׳—׳₪׳©  ׳׳× ׳”׳“׳¨׳ ׳׳”׳—׳“׳™׳¨ ׳׳—׳™׳™׳ ׳• ׳׳×

׳˜׳¨׳ ׳ ׳‘׳¨׳¨ ׳”׳“׳‘׳¨׳™׳, ׳ ׳§׳“׳™׳ ׳׳–׳” ׳׳× ׳׳׳׳¨׳• ׳”׳ ׳•׳“׳¢ ׳©׳ ׳”׳—׳›׳: "׳×׳›׳׳™׳× ׳”׳™׳“׳™׳¢׳” ׳©׳ ׳“׳¢ ׳©׳׳ ׳ ׳“׳¢". ׳•׳׳׳׳¨׳• ׳×׳׳•׳” ׳׳׳•׳“ ׳‘׳×׳׳×:   ׳.        ׳׳™׳ ׳™׳×׳›׳ ׳©׳”׳×׳›׳׳™׳× ׳©׳׳ ׳ ׳“׳¢, ׳•׳”׳¨׳™ ׳”׳“׳‘׳¨ ׳‘׳¨׳•׳¨ ׳•׳׳•׳¡׳›׳ ׳׳¦׳ ׳›׳ ׳—׳›׳׳™ ׳”׳×׳•׳¨׳” ׳•׳”׳׳•׳¡׳¨, ׳©׳¢׳ ׳”׳׳“׳ ׳׳”׳™׳•׳× ׳‘׳¨ ׳“׳¢׳× ׳•׳׳ ׳—"׳• ׳—׳¡׳¨ ׳“׳¢׳×? ׳‘. ׳׳“׳•׳¢ ׳ ׳¦׳¨׳ ׳׳׳׳•׳“ ׳׳× ׳›׳ ׳”׳×׳•׳¨׳” ׳›׳•׳׳” ׳‘׳›׳“׳™ ׳׳”׳’׳™׳¢ ׳׳׳¦׳‘ ׳©׳ ׳”׳¢׳“׳¨ ׳“׳¢׳×, ׳׳¦׳‘ ׳–׳” ׳§׳™׳™׳ ׳׳¦׳ ׳›׳ ׳׳—׳“ ׳©׳׳ ׳§׳¨׳ ׳•׳׳ ׳©׳ ׳”? ׳’. ׳׳™׳ ׳׳₪׳©׳¨ ׳׳×׳•׳ ׳”׳“׳¢׳× ׳׳”׳’׳™׳¢ ׳׳”׳¢׳“׳¨ ׳“׳¢׳×?

׳›׳ ׳¨׳׳”, ׳©׳‘׳¢׳¦׳ ׳”׳׳“׳ ׳׳™׳ ׳• ׳™׳•׳“׳¢ ׳׳”׳™ ׳‘׳׳׳× "׳׳”׳‘׳× ׳”'", ׳׳׳ ׳©׳›׳©׳ ׳•׳›׳— ׳׳“׳¢׳× ׳©׳™׳©׳ ׳” ׳׳¦׳•׳” ׳׳׳”׳•׳‘ ׳׳× ׳”', ׳•׳›׳׳• ׳›׳ ׳¢׳™׳™׳ ׳׳¢׳˜ ׳‘׳׳•׳‘׳ ׳‘׳¡׳₪׳¨׳™׳ ׳”׳§' ׳‘׳¢׳ ׳™׳ ׳–׳”, ׳”׳•׳ ׳‘׳ ׳” ׳׳¢׳¦׳׳• ׳“׳׳•׳× ׳•׳×׳‘׳ ׳™׳× ׳׳׳¦׳•׳” ׳–׳• ׳›׳₪׳™ ׳©׳”׳¦׳˜׳™׳™׳¨׳” ׳‘׳“׳׳™׳•׳ ׳• ׳׳₪׳™ ׳”׳‘׳ ׳×׳• ׳•׳”׳©׳’׳•׳×׳™׳•, ׳•׳›׳ ׳”׳’׳™׳¢ ׳׳׳¡׳§׳ ׳” ׳©׳׳›׳ ׳”׳ ׳• ׳‘׳’׳“׳¨ "׳׳•׳”׳‘ ׳”'". 
׳׳›׳ ׳׳§׳•׳©׳˜׳ ׳“׳׳™׳׳×׳ ׳›׳ ׳”׳‘׳ ׳™׳ ׳©׳‘׳ ׳” ׳׳¢׳¦׳׳•, ׳˜׳¢׳•׳× ׳”׳•׳ ׳׳™׳¡׳•׳“׳•, ׳׳׳—׳¨ ׳•׳׳™׳ ׳‘׳™׳“׳• ׳׳× ׳”׳›׳׳™׳ ׳”׳׳×׳׳™׳׳™׳ ׳׳‘׳ ׳•׳× ׳‘׳ ׳™׳ ׳׳¢׳™׳ ׳–׳”, ׳׳׳ ׳©׳‘׳׳§׳•׳ ׳׳”׳›׳™׳¨ ׳‘׳¢׳•׳‘׳“׳” ׳©׳׳™׳ ׳• ׳׳‘׳™׳ ׳׳”׳™ ׳׳”׳‘׳× ׳”', ׳”׳•׳ ׳‘׳•׳ ׳” ׳׳• ׳‘׳ ׳™׳ ׳©׳ ׳”׳‘׳ ׳•׳× ׳¢׳¦׳׳™׳•׳×, ׳•׳¢׳•׳“ ׳׳‘׳™׳ ׳׳”׳ ׳¡׳׳ ׳׳“׳‘׳¨׳™ ׳—׳–"׳, ׳•׳›׳“׳‘׳¨׳™ ׳”׳¨׳׳—"׳ <span style="color=#0055ff"><small>(׳‘׳₪׳¨׳§ ׳”׳ "׳)</small></span> "׳©׳ ׳¨׳׳” ׳׳”׳ ׳׳׳¦׳•׳ ׳¨׳׳™׳•׳× ׳’׳“׳•׳׳•׳× ׳•׳ ׳¡׳™׳•׳ ׳•׳× ׳׳•׳›׳™׳—׳™׳ ׳׳¡׳‘׳¨׳•׳×׳™׳”׳ ׳”׳¨׳¢׳•׳× ׳•׳׳“׳¢׳•׳×׳™׳”׳ ׳”׳›׳•׳–׳‘׳•׳×, ׳•׳–׳׳× ׳”׳™׳ ׳”׳¨׳¢׳” ׳”׳’׳“׳•׳׳” ׳”׳׳׳₪׳₪׳×׳ ׳•׳׳‘׳™׳׳×׳ ׳׳ ׳‘׳׳¨ ׳©׳—׳×". 
׳‘׳“׳‘׳¨׳™׳ ׳׳׳• ׳”׳©׳×׳“׳׳ ׳• ׳׳‘׳׳¨ ׳׳”׳™ ׳ ׳§׳•׳“׳× ׳”׳©׳§׳¨, ׳׳•׳׳ ׳›׳“׳™ ׳׳–׳›׳•׳× ׳׳”׳’׳™׳¢ ׳׳ ׳§׳•׳“׳× ׳”׳׳׳× ׳›׳‘׳¨ ׳׳™׳׳“׳ ׳• ׳‘׳¢׳ ׳”׳׳¡"׳™ [׳₪׳¨׳§ ׳’'] ׳›׳™ "׳׳ ׳׳•׳×׳ ׳©׳›׳‘׳¨ ׳™׳¦׳׳• ׳׳ ׳”׳׳׳¡׳¨ ׳”׳–׳”, ׳”׳ ׳¨׳•׳׳™׳ ׳”׳׳׳× ׳׳׳׳™׳×׳• ׳•׳™׳›׳•׳׳™׳ ׳׳™׳™׳¢׳¥ ׳©׳׳¨ ׳‘׳ ׳™ ׳׳“׳ ׳¢׳׳™׳•". ׳•׳¢׳ ׳׳ ׳©׳™׳ ׳”׳׳¡׳•׳’׳׳™׳ ׳׳™׳™׳¢׳¥ ׳׳׳—׳¨׳™׳ ׳•׳›׳׳•׳×׳, ׳›׳‘׳¨ ׳׳׳¨ ׳¨׳©׳‘"׳™ "׳¨׳׳™׳×׳™ ׳‘׳ ׳™ ׳¢׳׳™׳” ׳•׳”׳ ׳׳•׳¢׳˜׳™׳". 
׳•׳¢׳׳™׳ ׳• ׳׳“׳¢׳× ׳›׳™ ׳›׳©׳׳“׳ ׳׳™׳ ׳• ׳–׳›׳׳™, ׳›׳‘׳¨ ׳׳™׳׳“׳•׳ ׳• ׳—׳–"׳ "׳©׳”׳§׳‘"׳” ׳׳›׳©׳™׳׳ ׳‘׳‘׳ ׳™ ׳׳“׳ ׳©׳׳™׳ ׳ ׳׳”׳•׳’׳ ׳™׳". ׳•׳›׳ ׳׳¦׳™׳ ׳• ׳‘׳’׳' ׳‘"׳§ [׳ ׳‘ ׳¢"׳]: "׳›׳“ ׳¨׳’׳™׳– ׳¨׳¢׳™׳ ׳¢׳ ׳¢׳ ׳ ׳¢׳‘׳™׳“ ׳׳ ׳’׳“׳ ׳¡׳׳•׳×׳".

׳‘׳¦׳•׳¨׳” ׳–׳׳× ׳§׳ ׳” ׳‘׳₪׳ ׳™׳׳™׳•׳× ׳ ׳₪׳©׳• ׳׳× ׳¢׳ ׳™׳ ׳”׳™׳¨׳׳”. ׳׳™׳ ׳“׳‘׳¨׳™׳ ׳׳׳•׳¨׳™׳ ׳“׳•׳§׳ ׳‘׳§׳ ׳™׳× ׳׳“׳× ׳”׳™׳¨׳׳”, ׳׳׳ ׳‘׳›׳ ׳¢׳ ׳™׳ ׳•׳¢׳ ׳™׳ ׳¨׳•׳—׳ ׳™ ׳©׳׳™׳ ׳”׳—׳•׳© ׳”׳’׳©׳׳™ ׳™׳›׳•׳ ׳׳”׳©׳™׳’׳•, ׳¢׳ ׳”׳׳“׳ ׳׳—׳₪׳© ׳׳¢׳¦׳׳• ׳“׳•׳’׳׳ ׳׳¢׳™׳ ׳–׳” ׳‘׳¢׳•׳׳ ׳”׳’׳©׳׳™ ׳”׳׳•׳—׳©׳™, ׳•׳׳×׳•׳ ׳“׳•׳’׳׳ ׳–׳• ׳¢׳׳™׳• ׳׳”׳¢׳׳™׳§ ׳•׳׳”׳×׳‘׳•׳ ׳ ׳׳׳•׳“ ׳©׳׳™׳ ׳—׳™׳׳•׳§ ׳›׳׳ ׳‘׳™׳ ׳”׳¢׳•׳׳ ׳”׳’׳©׳׳™ ׳׳¢׳•׳׳ ׳”׳¨׳•׳—׳ ׳™. ׳‘׳•׳“׳׳™ ׳׳™׳ ׳–׳• ׳¢׳‘׳•׳“׳” ׳§׳׳”, ׳׳•׳׳ "׳׳“׳ ׳׳¢׳׳ ׳™׳•׳׳“", ׳׳“׳ ׳׳•׳›׳¨׳— ׳׳¢׳©׳•׳× ׳›׳ ׳¢׳“ ׳׳©׳¨ ׳™׳¨׳’׳™׳© ׳©׳”׳”׳•׳™׳” ׳”׳’׳©׳׳™׳× ׳•׳”׳”׳•׳™׳” ׳”׳¨׳•׳—׳ ׳™׳× ׳׳₪׳—׳•׳× ׳©׳•׳™׳ ׳”׳ ׳–׳” ׳׳–׳”, ׳›׳©׳ ׳©׳׳¦׳™׳׳•׳× ׳’׳©׳׳™׳× ׳”׳™׳ ׳׳¦׳™׳׳•׳× ׳’׳׳•׳¨׳” ׳׳—׳׳•׳˜׳™׳ ׳›׳ ׳׳¦׳™׳׳•׳× ׳¨׳•׳—׳ ׳™׳× ׳”׳™׳ ׳׳¦׳™׳׳•׳× ׳’׳׳•׳¨׳” ׳׳—׳׳•׳˜׳™׳ ׳׳  ׳₪׳—׳•׳×.
